info:King Guest Room
info:Stayed in June 2024
info:Couples
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 5, 2024
msg:Five-star experience, trip to Hampton by Hilton Xintang
Recently, I had the honor of staying at Hampton by Hilton Xintang. This is not just a simple accommodation experience, but also a comprehensive five-star enjoyment. From the moment I stepped into the hotel lobby, I was deeply attracted by the professional service and elegant environment here.
Lobby reception: As soon as I entered the lobby, the warm lighting and spacious space made me feel very comfortable. The service attitude of the front desk receptionist was extremely enthusiastic, and the smiling service was throughout. They not only checked in quickly and accurately, but also took the initiative to introduce me to the various facilities and services of the hotel, which made me feel very considerate.
Room experience: Walking into the guest room, the spacious and bright space design makes people shine. The room is fully equipped, and the bed is soft and comfortable, which makes me sleep well all night. It is particularly worth mentioning that the hygiene in the room is very good, and every place is clean and tidy, which makes people feel at ease. In addition, the sound insulation effect in the room is also quite good, and a quiet rest environment can be guaranteed even in the middle of the night.
Catering service: The hotel's restaurant offers a variety of food options, whether it is breakfast or dinner, it can meet the different tastes of guests. The restaurant's service staff is professional and attentive. They not only provide guests with delicious meals, but also take the initiative to ask guests about their taste preferences and recommend suitable dishes accordingly. In addition, the restaurant's environment is also very elegant, allowing people to enjoy a comfortable atmosphere while dining.
Fitness and Leisure: For guests who like fitness, the hotel's gym is definitely a place not to be missed. The equipment is complete and advanced, meeting the fitness needs of different guests. Let guests find a good place to relax during their busy journey.
Conference and Business: For business guests, the hotel's conference room and business center are equally excellent. The conference room is equipped with advanced audio and projection equipment to meet the needs of various business meetings. The business center provides one-stop services such as printing, copying, and faxing, allowing business guests to handle various affairs more conveniently.
Safety and Security: The hotel has also done a very good job in security. Whether it is the security staff at the front desk or the service staff in the guest rooms, they have undergone rigorous training to ensure the safety of the guests. At the same time, the hotel is also equipped with advanced monitoring systems and fire protection facilities to provide guests with a safe and reliable accommodation environment.
Other details: In addition to the above aspects, the hotel has also done an excellent job in details. For example, the mini bar in the room provides a variety of drinks and snacks for guests to choose from; the hotel also provides free WiFi service; the toiletries in the room also use high-quality brands... These details make guests feel the sincerity and quality of the hotel.
Overall, I was deeply impressed by Hampton by Hilton Xintang. Whether it is from the service, facilities, environment or details, it shows a five-star level. I believe that this stay experience will become one of the good memories of my trip. If you are looking for a high-quality and comfortable accommodation option, then Hampton by Hilton Xintang is definitely a place worth recommending!

msg:This Hampton Hilton actually charges you for staying after 2 o'clock. Oh my god, I won't consider this hotel again.
The location is also remote. If you are not familiar with driving, you will often miss the intersection and go around. Even if you drive there for the second time, you will go around the wrong intersection. There are a bunch of construction sites nearby and roads are being built, and smoke and dust are billowing. No wonder reservations at this hotel are often non-cancellable. Other hotels can cancel for free in the evening or noon on the day of check-in.
The breakfast tastes similar to that in nearby Vienna, with no highlights, but in Vienna, breakfast for two people is 300 yuan, and this one costs more than 400 yuan, which is expensive and average. In addition, if you can‚Äôt finish the breakfast in Vienna, you can take it away. Also, the TV screen projection in the room didn't work.
The air conditioner only has air conditioning but no heating. I called the front desk and found out that it wasn't broken. It just didn't have heating. Is the heating function just a decoration...
The second waiter contacted me later, and the service was also extremely poor. He only tried to shirk responsibility.
I have stayed at Hampton Hilton so many times, but I have never had such a bad experience. I feel very bad.



The check-out experience was very bad. On the day of check-out, I was taking a nap and overslept. When I slept until 1:30, the front desk suddenly called me and asked if I wanted to extend my stay. If I didn't extend my stay, my stay would be deducted after 2 o'clock. I was so scared that I immediately got up and packed my things. It was already 1:50. I finished packing, but my girlfriend was still a little slow, so I took the room card, thinking about returning the room card, checking out the room, and then coming up to the room to help my daughter. Friends, let's take the luggage. Fortunately, at the last moment, I looked at my watch and paid off the room card at 1:59, and was about to go to the elevator to help my girlfriend get her luggage, but I couldn't get in without the room card. I tried for a long time but couldn't get up. I didn‚Äôt answer the phone call. I found out later that after I pulled out the room key card, the curtains would automatically close and the whole room would be dark. My girlfriend packed her things in the darkness and then took her large and small bags to the front desk in a very embarrassed manner. It was such a bad experience that I was not in the mood to play in the afternoon.
It's too bad. Although everything was in order before check-out, I didn't expect that I would be charged for exceeding the check-out time. Quan Ji, who used to live next door, overslept at noon. The most he could do was make a few more phone calls to remind me. It‚Äôs okay to ask for multiple good reviews. Vienna, where I live nearby, didn't even bother to remind me of the timeout.
